async function inspectListing2(item, idx) {
  const u = `https://www.airbnb.com/rooms/${item.id}?adults=2&check_in=2026-05-15&check_out=2026-05-18&children=2&pets=1&search_mode=regular_search&amenities%5B%5D=9&amenities%5B%5D=33`;
  const tab = await openTab(u);
  await tab.waitForLoadState('domcontentloaded').catch(()=>{});
  // wait until the title or amenities text appears
  for (let i=0; i<8; i++) {
    const txt0 = await tab.locator('body').innerText().catch(e=>'');
    if (txt0.includes('What this place offers') || txt0.includes(item.name.split('|')[0].trim()) || txt0.length > 2000) break;
    await sleep(1000);
  }
  const snap = await snapshot(tab);
  const body = await tab.locator('body').innerText().catch(e=>'');
  const lower = body.toLowerCase();
  const gymTerms = ['gym','fitness','workout','exercise'];
  const mentions = gymTerms.filter(t => lower.includes(t));
  const gymContexts = [];
  for (const t of gymTerms) {
    let pos = lower.indexOf(t);
    if (pos >= 0) gymContexts.push(body.slice(Math.max(0,pos-120), Math.min(body.length,pos+180)).replace(/\s+/g,' '));
  }
  // collect visible amenities segment if present
  const amenitiesMatch = body.match(/What this place offers([\s\S]{0,700})/);
  await closeTab(tab);
  return {idx, ...item, url:u, bodyLen:body.length, mentions, gymContexts, amenitiesSnippet: amenitiesMatch ? amenitiesMatch[0].replace(/\s+/g,' ') : null, title: await tab.title().catch(e=>'closed')};
}
const inspectResults = [];
for (let i=0; i<relaxedListings.length; i++) {
  const res = await inspectListing2(relaxedListings[i], i+1).catch(e=>({idx:i+1, name:relaxedListings[i].name, error:String(e)}));
  inspectResults.push(res);
  console.log(JSON.stringify(res));
}
page = tabs[0];

<request>
const exactAll3 = [
  {name:'Lakeview Penthouse + Modern + Rooftop + Parking', id:'1671947189812529172', listed:'Apartment in Cleveland', total:1487, rating:'New place to stay'},
  {name:'Beautiful historic home - Gordon Sq. Arts District', id:'1887015', listed:'Home in Cleveland', total:2243, rating:'4.76, 96 reviews'}
];
async function inspectListingExact(item) {
  const url = `https://www.airbnb.com/rooms/${item.id}?adults=2&check_in=2026-05-15&check_out=2026-05-18&children=2&pets=1&amenities%5B%5D=9&amenities%5B%5D=33&amenities%5B%5D=15`;
  const tab = await openTab(url);
  await tab.waitForLoadState('domcontentloaded').catch(()=>{});
  for (let i=0;i<10;i++) {
    const body = await tab.locator('body').innerText().catch(e=>'');
    if (body.includes('What this place offers') && body.includes('Reserve')) break;
    await tab.mouse.wheel(0, 900).catch(()=>{});
    await sleep(800);
  }
  const snap = await snapshot(tab);
  console.log('SNAPSHOT_FOR ' + item.name + '\n' + snap.tree);
  const body = await tab.locator('body').innerText().catch(e=>'');
  const amenitiesSnippet = (body.match(/What this place offers[\s\S]{0,1000}/)||[''])[0].replace(/\s+/g,' ');
  const gymContexts = [];
  const lower = body.toLowerCase();
  for (const term of ['gym','fitness','workout','exercise']) {
    let idx = lower.indexOf(term);
    if (idx>=0) gymContexts.push(body.slice(Math.max(0, idx-150), Math.min(body.length, idx+220)).replace(/\s+/g,' '));
  }
  const locationMatch = (body.match(/Where you’ll be[\s\S]{0,250}/)||[''])[0].replace(/\s+/g,' ');
  const result = { ...item, url, amenitiesSnippet, gymContexts, locationMatch };
  await closeTab(tab);
  return result;
}
const exactDetails = [];
for (const item of exactAll3) {
  const r = await inspectListingExact(item);
  exactDetails.push(r);

}
